 she was the reason why i joined wattpad and why my stories existed . 
 about the author m.g. marquez is a third year bs accountancy student at batangas state university . 
 she is a lover of tragedy and has always been fascinated with death . 
 she mostly writes under the influence of songs , and is inspired with first-hand and second-hand experiences . 
 she is an active member of wattpad.com as gulliblegummybear .
